match(a:tag where name = '其他')-[e]-(b:user) return a.value, b.name
match(a:account where n.name=XiaoHu)-[e:friend]->{1,2}(b:account) return b
match(a where a.name='马建国')-[e:relation]->(b where b.createTime <> '2023-01-06' and b.lang <> 'English') return b.wordCount,e.timeStamp, e.f1
match(a where a.name='黄国强')-[e]->(b:medicine)<-[e2]-(c where c.name='杜建聪') return b limit 50
a.height * 152
with p as (select * from (VALUES('四川大学',1,142),('北京大学',3,952),('中国科技大学',4,691),('四川大学',1,161)) as t(name,level,value))MATCH (a WHERE a.name = p.name AND (a.name = '伦敦')) -[e:city_contain_company ]->(b:company WHERE b.name <> '阿里' AND b.value IS NOT NULL) RETURN b LIMIT 168
match(a:student) return a.salary group by a.height order by a.salary desc
match(a:user) return a
match(a:person) return a.salary group by a.height, a.salary, a.name order by a.salary asc
match(a:person where a.id = 4)-[e:watch]->(b:film) let b.value = AVG((b:film)-[e2]-(c:comment) => c.id) match(b:film where b.value < 4)-[e3:has]->(d:tag) return b.value, d
match(a:person where a.name='黄建国')-[e]-(b:person) return b.gender
match(a:software where name = 'Hive')-[e:uses]->(b:software)<-[e2:commits]-(c:person) return b, c
with p as (select * from (VALUES(967),(191),(752),(258),(35)) as t(id)) MATCH (a WHERE a.id = p.id AND (a.name = '大众影院')) -[e:cinema_releases_film ]->(b:film) RETURN b
